<dl><dd><i>On ne se souvient plus <a href = vnd.unilang:des.html>des</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:promesses.html>promesses</a>, quand <a href = vnd.unilang:les.html>les</a> périls <a href = vnd.unilang:sont.html>sont</a> passés</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:zegt.html>zegt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> fransche <a href = vnd.unilang:spreekwoord.html>spreekwoord</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:motto.html>motto</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Algerijnen <a href = vnd.unilang:immer.html>immer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schreven.html>schreven</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> teboekstellen <a href = vnd.unilang:hunner.html>hunner</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verdragen.html>verdragen</a>; want by <a href = vnd.unilang:iedere.html>iedere</a> verademing, <a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a> eene ontfangene tuchtiging, <b>schuimden</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> Korsaren den <a href = vnd.unilang:oceaan.html>Oceaan</a> roofgieriger <b><a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ooit.html>ooit</a>.
<dl><dd><i>One no longer follows through on promises, when the threats have passed</i>, says the French proverb: it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> the <i><a href = vnd.unilang:motto.html>motto</a></i> that the Algerians always <a href = vnd.unilang:wrote.html>wrote</a> on the codifications of their treaties; for during every respite, after a received punitive expedition, those Corsairs <b>plundered</b> the ocean more rapaciously than ever.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2010</b>, Jan Cremer, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hunnen.html>Hunnen</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:bezig.html>Bezige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>Bij</a>, 754.
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> <b>schuimden</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:straten.html>straten</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:kwamen.html>kwamen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vooral.html>vooral</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:donker.html>donker</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schuilplaatsen.html>schuilplaatsen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tevoorschijn.html>tevoorschijn</a>.
<dl><dd>They <b>plundered</b> the streets, and <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> out of their hiding <a href = vnd.unilang:places.html>places</a> mostly under the cover of darkness.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2014</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:kate.html>Kate</a> Williams, <i> Joséphine. <a href = vnd.unilang:verlangen.html>Verlangen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ambitie.html>ambitie</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:napoleon.html>Napoleon</a></i>, Prometheus.
<dl><dd>Roversbendes <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zakkenrollers.html>zakkenrollers</a> <b>schuimden</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:straten.html>straten</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moorden.html>moorden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waren.html>waren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:orde.html>orde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dag.html>dag</a>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:afschuwelijk.html>afschuwelijk</a> (2856)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">afschuwen</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-lijk</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:afschuwelijk.html>afschuwelijk</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:afschuwelijk.html>afschuwelijker</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">afschuwelijkst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>heinous, horrible</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:afschuwelijk.html>afschuwelijk</a></strong>
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">afslaen</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slaan.html>slaan</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:afslaan.html>afslaan</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to decline, to reject</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to <a href = vnd.unilang:halt.html>halt</a>, to <a href = vnd.unilang:stop.html>stop</a>, to switch off
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:motor.html>motor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:afgeslagen.html>afgeslagen</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The engine <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:turned.html>turned</a> off</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to turn, to take off in a direction perpendicular to the one one <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> travelling in before</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to strike off</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to beat up

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">afslach</i>. <p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:afstraffen.html>afstraffen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to punish (severely)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-ing, -ion, -ment</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A severe punishment, usually as retribution.</li>
<li>A memorable lesson <span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(<span id="rfv-sense-notice-nl-"></span>Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> verify<sup class="plainlinks">(<a class="external text" href="https://en.wiktionary.org/w/index.php?title=Wiktionary:Requests_for_verification/Non-Englishamp;action=editamp;section=newamp;preload=Template:rfv-sense/preloadamp;preloadtitle=%5B%5Bafstraffing%23rfv-sense-notice-nl-%7cafstraffing%5D%5D">+</a>)</sup> this sense?)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>Die</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:afstraffing.html>afstraffing</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:zullen.html>zullen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gauw.html>gauw</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vergeten.html>vergeten</a>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">They <a href = vnd.unilang:won.html>won</a>'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> forget that lesson in a long time!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>A painful, embarrassing failure or defeat, a beating.

***afstrijken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:afstrijken.html>afstrijken</a> (109869)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">afstriken</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:strijken.html>strijken</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:afstrijken.html>afstrijken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to strike <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a match, to attempt to ignite it</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> veiligheidslucifer, in tegensteling <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> strijklucifer, <a href = vnd.unilang:kun.html>kun</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:redelijk.html>redelijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:alles.html>alles</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:afstrijken.html>afstrijken</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">A safety match, as opposed to a strike-anywhere match, can'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> be easily <b>struck</b> on any surface.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to <span class="Latn" lang="en">rub out</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:strijk.html>Strijk</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:overvloed.html>overvloed</a> kit <b><a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> terpentine.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Rub out</b> excessive sealant with turpentine.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aftrekken.html>aftrekken</a> (9152)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">aftrecken</i>. The sense “to subtract” <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> coined by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Simon_Stevin" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Simon Stevin"><a href = vnd.unilang:simon.html>Simon</a> Stevin</a> as a calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">dētrahō</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:trekken.html>trekken</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aftrekken.html>aftrekken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pull off</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> arithmetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to subtract</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to clean/level etc. with a squeegee</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to wank, to <a href = vnd.unilang:jack.html>jack</a> off; to stimulate with one's hand of one's own or another one's <a href = vnd.unilang:penis.html>penis</a></li></ol>
